ain_Project/wiki/Catastrophic_interference/wiki/Cerebellar_Model_Articulation_Controller/wiki/Cognitive_architecture/wiki/Cognitive_science/wiki/Convolutional_neural_network/wiki/Connectionist_expert_system/wiki/Connectomics/wiki/Cultured_neuronal_networks/wiki/Deep_learning/wiki/Encog/wiki/Fuzzy_logic/wiki/Gene_expression_programming/wiki/Genetic_algorithm/wiki/Genetic_programming/wiki/Group_method_of_data_handling/wiki/Habituation/wiki/In_Situ_Adaptive_Tabulation/wiki/List_of_machine_learning_concepts/wiki/Models_of_neural_computation/wiki/Neuroevolution/wiki/Neural_coding/wiki/Neural_gas/wiki/Neural_machine_translation/wiki/Neural_network_software/wiki/Neuroscience/wiki/Nonlinear_system_identification/wiki/Optical_neural_network/wiki/Parallel_Constraint_Satisfaction_Processes/wiki/Parallel_distributed_processing/wiki/Radial_basis_function_network/wiki/Recurrent_neural_networks/wiki/Self-organizing_map/wiki/Spiking_neural_network/wiki/Systolic_array/wiki/Tensor_product_network/wiki/Time_delay_neural_network/w/index.php?title=Artificial_neural_network&action=edit&section=72#cite_ref-1/wiki/Digital_object_identifier//doi.org/10.1007%2FBF02478259#cite_ref-2https://www.degruyter.com/view/books/9781400882618/9781400882618-002/9781400882618-002.xml#cite_ref-3https://books.google.com/books?id=ddB4AgAAQBAJ/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number/wiki/Special:BookSources/978-1-135-63190-1#cite_ref-4/wiki/Digital_object_identifier//doi.org/10.1109%2FTIT.1954.1057468#cite_ref-5/wiki/Digital_object_identifier//doi.org/10.1109%2FTIT.1956.1056810#cite_ref-6/wiki/CiteSeerX//citeseerx.ist.psu.edu/viewdoc/summary?doi=10.1.1.588.3775/wiki/Digital_object_identifier//doi.org/10.1037%2Fh0042519/wiki/PubMed_Identifier//www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pubmed/13602029#cite_ref-Werbos_1975_7-0#cite_ref-Werbos_1975_7-1https://books.google.com/books?id=z81XmgEACAAJ#cite_ref-8https://books.google.com/books?id=8YrxWojxUA4C&pg=PA106/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number/wiki/Special:BookSources/978-0-1
